<userid>116927299349278480672<//userid>< Text>
They did great window tinting work but their customer service was less than great.  The front desk lady had an indifferent attitude and did not give me info on the difference between their products they offer.  I had to ask specific questions rather than her being informative and she would only answer my questions rather than elaborate on the product.  In the end they worked quickly and I was really happy with it but if you are going to go here, do your homework first and know what type of film you want before you get there.  I would recommend this place for window tinting.</Text>

It said older cars (2005 and older) will be charged more for tinting the windows. I already paid $88.00 with Groupon but when I called they wanted another $76.00 to do the work. I asked the guy on the phone why so much and why does it cost more for older cars. He told me they charge more because they have to do extra cleaning on the windows. $76.00 more just to clean the windows???? Are you kidding me??  The Groupon fine print also said to call a week ahead of time so I could get my car in.
This company must way over book because they couldn't get my car in until 8/23. I am NOT waiting 20 days. Anyway this company just lost a long time customer and I think this place needs to pull their add from Groupon if they can't keep up. Very poor customer service Groupon did give me a full refund..</Review>

< Review>
What a gem to have found in Dixon! We make the trip from Suisun City at least a couple of times a month to enjoy the relaxed atmosphere, great service and food so good that one would be hard pressed to find anything better in San Francisco or Napa! And the prices are beyond reasonable for the creative and changing menu.

Chef Wyatt is young and energetic as well as enthusiastic and talented. On Thursdays, he creates a tasting menu using the locally grown, farmers market selections. I have tried something different on each visit and have yet to be anything but pleasantly happy to benefit from his thoughtful creations. I‚Äôll be bringing friends there this Saturday to dine on our way to Thunder Valley to see Ron White perform.

I heartily recommend that anyone interested in a great meal served in a great atmosphere at great prices, make the 5 minute drive off Interstate 80 at the central Dixon exit. Just be prepared to find reasons to drive that stretch of the freeway often, just to have an excuse to exit there and go to Dawson‚Äôs!< /Review>
